    <script type="text/javascript">
    // cambiar fecha del contador 
        (function () {
        const second = 1000,
        minute = second * 60,
        hour = minute * 60,
        day = hour * 24;

        let today = new Date(),
        dd = String(today.getDate()).padStart(2, "0"),
        mm = String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, "0"),
        yyyy = today.getFullYear(),
        nextYear = yyyy,
        dayMonth = "09/29/", // MM/DD
        birthday = dayMonth + yyyy;

        today = mm + "/" + dd + "/" + yyyy;
        if (today > birthday) {
        birthday = dayMonth + nextYear;
        }
        // end

        const countDown = new Date(birthday).getTime(),
        x = setInterval(function () {
            const now = new Date().getTime(),
            distance = countDown - now;

            (document.getElementById("countdown-days").innerText = Math.floor(
            distance / day
            )),
            (document.getElementById("countdown-hours").innerText = Math.floor(
                (distance % day) / hour
            )),
            (document.getElementById("countdown-minutes").innerText = Math.floor(
                (distance % hour) / minute
            )),
            (document.getElementById("countdown-seconds").innerText = Math.floor(
                (distance % minute) / second
            ));
        }, 0);
    })();
    </script>

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const hideWspDiv = document.getElementById("pr-web-whatsapp");
    if (hideWspDiv) {
        let currentPath = window.location.pathname;
        if (currentPath.startsWith('/')) {
            currentPath = currentPath.substring(1); 
        }
        
        const shouldHide = noWspURL.some(route => {
            if (route.endsWith('/')) {
                return currentPath.startsWith(route);
            } else {
                return currentPath === route || currentPath === (route + '/');
            }
        });
        if (shouldHide) {
            hideWspDiv.style.display = 'none';
            const scrollToTopButton = document.querySelector('.ast-scroll-to-top-right');
            
            if (scrollToTopButton) {
                scrollToTopButton.style.bottom = '90px';
            }
        }
    }
});
/* End hide WSP urls */

   document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
     var bookNowLinks = document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="https://book.perurail.com/"]');
     bookNowLinks.forEach(function(link) {
       var observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
         mutations.forEach(function(mutation) {
           if (mutation.type === 'attributes' && mutation.attributeName === 'href') {
             var href = link.getAttribute('href');
             // Elimina cualquier ocurrencia de dos puntos consecutivos
             if (href.includes('..')) {
               href = href.replace(/\.\./g, '');
               link.setAttribute('href', href);
             }
             if (href.includes('..')) {
            href = href.replace(/\.\./g, '');
            link.setAttribute('href', href);
          }
          if (href.endsWith('.') || href.endsWith('..')) {
            href = href.slice(0, -2);
            link.setAttribute('href', href);
          }             
           }
         });
       });
       
       observer.observe(link, {
         attributes: true // Monitorea cambios en los atributos
       });
     });
